[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mA Jazzer-based fuzzing run of the `TikaAppUntarringFuzzer` harness against Apache [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mTika’s `TikaUntar` CLI has triggered a critical security finding: a file path [0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mtraversal vulnerability. The sanitizer detected that entries extracted by [0m          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`TikaUntar` could escape the intended output directory and write to arbitrary [0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mlocations on the filesystem. [0m                                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m## Description[0m                                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Issue observed  [0m                                                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  During an automated fuzzing session, the harness invoked [0m                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`[0m[1;35morg.apache.tika.cli.TikaUntar.main[0m[1;39m([0m[33m...[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` with a maliciously crafted TAR archive [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;39m([0m[39m`[0m[35m/[0m[95mtestcase[0m[39m`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m. As the code processed archive entries, the FilePathTraversal [0m        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39msanitizer raised a `FuzzerSecurityIssueCritical` exception, indicating that a path [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39msuch as  [0m                                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  ```[0m                                                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  [0m[35m/tmp/[0m[95mexpander-tmp[0m[39m*[0m[35m/output/q/r/[0m[95mjazzer-traversal[0m                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  ```  [0m                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  would be written outside the allowed extraction directory.[0m                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Vulnerability type  [0m                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  File path traversal [0m[35m/[0m[39m directory traversal vulnerability in archive extraction.[0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Important observations and findings  [0m                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  • The sanitizer hook [0m                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`com.code_intelligence.jazzer.sanitizers.FilePathTraversal.pathFirstArgHook` [0m       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mintervened in `TikaUntar.main`, stopping execution once an out-of-bounds path was [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mdetected.  [0m                                                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  • The crash occurred before any actual write, purely at the path validation [0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mstage.  [0m                                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  • Relevant sanitizer stack frames:  [0m                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m    – [0m[1;35mFilePathTraversal.check[0m[1;39m([0m[33m...[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m  [0m                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m    – [0m[1;35mFilePathTraversal.pathFirstArgHook[0m[1;39m([0m[33m...[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m  [0m                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m    – [0m[1;35morg.apache.tika.cli.TikaUntar.main[0m[1;39m([0m[33m...[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m  [0m                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  • The harness code [0m[1;39m([0m[39m`TikaAppUntarringFuzzer.parseOne` → `fuzzerTestOneInput`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39msimply forwards the raw input file to `TikaUntar`.  [0m                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Parts of the codebase to investigate  [0m                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  [0m[1;36m1[0m[39m. `org.apache.tika.cli.TikaUntar` – entry point for TAR extraction, argument [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mhandling, and file creation logic.  [0m                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  [0m[1;36m2[0m[39m. Underlying stream processing in [0m                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`org.apache.commons.compress.archivers.tar.TarArchiveInputStream` and related [0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mutility classes, to see how entry names are sanitized [0m[1;39m([0m[39mor not[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m.  [0m                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  [0m[1;36m3[0m[39m. Any helper methods in Tika that resolve output file paths [0m[1;39m([0m[39me.g., path joining,[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mcanonicalization[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m.  [0m                                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  [0m[1;36m4[0m[39m. The fuzzing harness [0m[1;39m([0m[39m`com.example.TikaAppUntarringFuzzer`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m to confirm it does [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mnot impose additional path restrictions beyond Tika’s own code.[0m                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m## Initial Issue Log[0m                                                                [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m         [39mA patch was applied to `TikaUntar.java` to guard against traversal by:[0m              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Normalizing the extraction directory [0m[1;39m([0m[39m`extractDir`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m.[0m                              [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- The fuzzer command runs `TikaAppUntarringFuzzer` against `[0m[35m/[0m[95mtestcase[0m[39m`, exercising [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`[0m[1;35mTikaUntar.main[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m`.[0m                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- During archive extraction, a file entry with path components like [0m                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`q/r/jazzer-traversal` [0m[1;39m([0m[39mor `..[0m[35m/../[0m[95mjazzer-traversal[0m[39m`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m escapes the intended output [0m   [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  ```[0m                                                                               [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  ```[0m                                                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- This sanitizer-triggered exception aborts the process with exit status [0m[1;36m77[0m[39m.[0m        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### Key Observations in the Initial Log[0m                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- The harness code [0m[1;39m([0m[39m`TikaAppUntarringFuzzer`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m is simply invoking `TikaUntar.main` [0m  [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### Patch Attempt[0m                                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mIn `tika-app/src/main/java/org/apache/tika/cli/TikaUntar.java`, the code in the [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mfile extraction loop was modified:[0m                                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mOriginal snippet:[0m                                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m```[0m                                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mPath target = [0m[1;35mextractDir.resolve[0m[1;39m([0m[1;35mtae.getName[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[1;39m)[0m[1;35m.normalize[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m```[0m                                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mPatch changes:[0m                                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m```[0m                                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mPath normalizedExtractDir = [0m[1;35mextractDir.toAbsolutePath[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[1;35m.normalize[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mPath target = [0m[1;35mnormalizedExtractDir.resolve[0m[1;39m([0m[1;35mtae.getName[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[1;39m)[0m[1;35m.normalize[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mif [0m[1;39m([0m[39m![0m[1;35mtarget.startsWith[0m[1;39m([0m[39mnormalizedExtractDir[0m[1;39m)[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m[1;39m{[0m                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m    throw new [0m[1;35mIOException[0m[1;39m([0m[32m"Path traversal attempt detected: "[0m[39m + [0m[1;35mtae.getName[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;39m}[0m                                                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m```[0m                                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- `normalizedExtractDir` is computed once from `extractDir`.[0m                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Each entry’s name [0m[1;39m([0m[39m`[0m[1;35mtae.getName[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m is resolved against `normalizedExtractDir` [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mand normalized.[0m                                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- A `startsWith` check enforces that `target` remains within [0m                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`normalizedExtractDir`.[0m                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- An explicit `IOException` is thrown on violation.[0m                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### Log After Patch[0m                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### Areas for Further Investigation[0m                                                 [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m4[0m[39m. **Normalization of `extractDir`**  [0m                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Confirm that `[0m[1;35mtoAbsolutePath[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[1;35m.normalize[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` covers all relative path cases and[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39msymbolic link resolution if applicable.[0m                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m5[0m[39m. **Integration with Jazzer Sanitizers**  [0m                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Determine if manual checks and Jazzer’s FilePathTraversal sanitizer overlap or[0m [2m                [0m
